Our catalog with **#20250201** (Catalog version **3.4.303** ) is available to our **Easy2Patch** customers.

This week, **61** software updates are provided in the E2P catalog. We support **446** products of **288** individual manufacturers in total. We are updating **587** products with 32/64-bit and language options.

***Note:*** *VirusTotal and Kaspersky Opentip scans are the responsibility of the manufacturer. E2P Bilisim has no responsibility or liability for the virus scanning results of the files.*

After setting the expiry date, select “Set expiry alert” and choose an alert schedule from the dropdown menu. > Change Log for Amazon Corretto 17 The following sections describe the changes for each release of Amazon Corretto 17. Corretto version: 17.0.14.7.1 Release Date: January 21, 2025 Target Platforms 1 RPM-based Linux using glibc 2.12 or later, x86, x86\_64 Debian-based Linux using glibc 2.12 or later, x86, x86\_64 RPM-based Linux using glibc 2.17 or later, aarch64

> Changes in MySQL Connector/ODBC 9.2.0 Bugs Fixed The user defined traceparent query attribute in an OpenTelemetry instrumented application was not sent to the server, which resulted in user (or connector) generated OpenTelemetry spans to not associate with the corresponding server spans. (Bug #37188732) References: This issue is a regression of: Bug #36841317. Retrieving a list of records that contained an empty BLOB field could return an unexpected result. (Bug #116657, Bug #37286526)

> 2024.4 This release includes a number of improvements in Microsoft Office, braille, and document formatting. In Word or Excel, it is now possible to double-press the comment gesture to read the comment or note in a browsable dialog. You can now use the review cursor selection command to select text in PowerPoint. NVDA also no longer brailles garbage characters when showing row or column header text in tables in Word when using the object model.
